 ullekhneey he ki jalwaayu parivartan ke falswaroop sardi, garmi or barish ke mausam kii avadhi main bhi badlaav spasht rup se dikh rahaa he

 1
 agar prashasan ko lagata he ki kisi kaa bandook yaa pistal ke license ko radd karnaa public ke hit or suraksha ke liye jaruri he, to vah radd kar saktaa he
 2
 jis vyakti ko bandook yaa pistal kaa license mila he, agar wo dimagi rup se disturb ho jaataa he, to prashasan uske license ko radd kar detaa he
 3
 agar kisi ne juthi jaankaree dekar yaa kisi jaankaree ko chhipaakar license hasil kiya he yani niyamon kaa ulanghan karke license hasil kiya he, to aise license ko radd kiya ja saktaa he
 4
 license kii sharton, arms act or arms rules ke kanoon kaa ulanghan hone par bhi license radd ho saktaa he
 5
 agar hathiyaar ko jamaa karne kaa nirdesh diya jaataa he or license rakhane vaala uskaa paalan karne main vifal rahata he, to bhi license ko radd karne kii karrwai kii ja sakati he
 6
 jiske naam license he, agar wo chaahe, to aavedan dekar apane license ko radd karvaa saktaa he
 7
 agar hoicourt arms kanoon kaa ulanghan paata he, to apni shaktiyon kaa istemaal karte hue bhi license radd kar saktaa he
 8
 centre sarkaar nirdesh par bhi hathiyaaron ke license ko radd karne kiya ja saktaa he
 9
 agar kisi ko arms act yaa arms rules ke tahat adaalat se sajaa mili he, to bhi uske license ko radd kiya ja saktaa he
